Annam Limits Immigration 23

Limit of 1,500 People per Country

(Tokyo) According to a telegram from the Consulate General in Batavia to the Japanese Ministry of Foreign Affairs, the Annam government proposed a draft decree on immigration at the Council on the 15th and does not allow it to be announced immediately. The content of the draft decree is to adopt a system of limiting the same number of immigrants from each country each year. If the total number of immigrants in that year is less than the prescribed number, it may exceed one-tenth of the total number of immigrants in the past ten years. The total number of immigrants is 25,000, and each country is limited to 1,500 people. The average total number of Japanese immigrants between 1923 and October 1932 was 821, so it has no direct impact on Japan, but it is feared that it will hinder future overseas development, so it is given great importance. (Dentsu News Agency, 17th)

Atlantic Shipping Competition

Italy's Newly Built Fast Ship 24

Travels at 29 Knots per Hour

Breaks the Record of German Ships

(New York) The Italian newly built steamship Rex recently crossed the Atlantic Ocean from Gibraltar to New York, setting a new record with a result of four days, thirteen hours, and fifty-eight minutes. The total distance reached 3,181 miles, and the average speed per hour was 29 nautical miles. According to the previous record holder, the German steamship Bremen, which sailed from New York to Cherbourg on June 30, the result was four days, sixteen hours, and fifteen minutes, and the average speed per hour was 28.51 nautical miles. (Reuters, 16th)

U.S. Recovery Plan Encounters Setbacks 25

Roosevelt Urges Steel Industry to Cooperate, 60,000 Men and Women Garment Workers Declare Strike

National News Agency, Washington, 16th - The U.S. President, seeing that his industrial recovery plan is facing real danger, met with the two leaders of the American steel industry who came to Beijing yesterday for a long talk. The U.S. President is deeply concerned about the attitude of the steel industry towards the recovery plan. However, according to people in the White House, the President still does not intend to use harsh means to force the industry to obey, but only wants the industry's full cooperation and wants to hear its opinions. It is expected that the President will persuade the two to give the government the necessary cooperation. As for the attitude of the representatives of the steel industry, it is said that they are also willing to cooperate, but they want to obtain an understanding of the government's position on organized labor. It is heard that the President assured today that the purpose of his industrial plan is only to improve the labor situation and that he has no intention of forcibly unifying the principles of labor in any industry. The steel industry was one of the first to submit industry rules. It is expected that the main objection of the industry is to certain conditions added to the industry rules, because it is believed that these conditions are initiated by Green. The government is also working hard to mediate the strike wave of coat and women's clothing workers because it is feared that it will indirectly affect the textile industry, which employs one million workers. Although the industrial recovery plan has encountered setbacks, according to statistics from the Department of Labor, the number of employees in July increased by 7.2% compared with June, and the total amount of wages paid also increased by 7.93%.

National News Agency, New York, 16th - After 2,500 coat tailors in New York City went on strike yesterday, 60,000 men and women garment workers in women's clothing factories in New York, New Jersey, and Connecticut went on strike today, claiming that they would not resume work until wages were increased and treatment was improved. Representatives from the U.S. Department of Labor and the Industrial Recovery Administration have been mediating for 48 hours without success. The most painful thing for coat workers is that most of them are not directly employed by manufacturers, so they are exploited by big and small contractors. Therefore, they demand the abolition of these intermediaries and direct employment by manufacturers. As for the workers employed in clothing factories, they claim that their wages are not enough to live on and that the treatment in most factories is harsh. Disputes in the coat industry have been going on for several months. Newly, 22,000 male coat tailors went on strike and were temporarily resolved. According to today's situation, it is feared that the strike wave will extend to other industries, such as fur and textile industries, which may be affected.

U.S. News Media Joins Industry Rules 26

Havas News Agency, Washington, 16th - Before the industry rules for the news media are finalized and adopted, the temporary industry rules set by the government continue to be in effect. Various newspapers have now joined the temporary industry rules and have been able to use the blue eagle, which represents national economic recovery, as a symbol.

Luo Wengan Inspects Xinjiang

President Wang Concurrently Assumes Duties of Foreign Minister and Minister of Justice, Vice Minister Zheng to Act on His Behalf 27

(Nanjing) The National Government issued an order on the 17th stating that Luo Wengan, Minister of Foreign Affairs and concurrently Minister of Judicial Administration, will go on a tour of Xinjiang. All duties of the Minister of Foreign Affairs will be concurrently assumed by Wang Zhaoming, President of the Executive Yuan, with immediate effect. [This is according to a Central News Agency dispatch on the 17th.]

(Nanjing) Since Huang Musong, the Central Government's envoy to comfort Xinjiang, returned to Nanjing and reported, the Central Government, considering Xinjiang's strategic border location, has appointed Liu Wenlong as Chairman and Sheng Shicai as Supervisor to ensure local affairs are managed. Regarding central government affairs such as foreign affairs and transportation, it is deeply felt that there is a need to dispatch senior officials for further inspection and separate handling. Chairman Chiang Kai-shek and President Wang Zhaoming have repeatedly requested President Dai Chuanxian of the Examination Yuan to go. President Dai therefore traveled quickly to Guling to discuss everything in person. However, due to his health not being fully recovered, it is difficult to travel long distances in the short term. Minister Luo of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs then agreed with Chairman Chiang Kai-shek and President Wang Zhaoming to personally inspect Xinjiang. A report was submitted at the political meeting on August 16th. During Minister Luo's inspection, the duties of the Minister of Foreign Affairs will be temporarily assumed by President Wang, while the duties of the Minister of Judicial Administration will be handled on behalf of him by Vice Minister Zheng. The political meeting has already approved it, and it is said that a clear order will be issued soon. [This is according to a Central News Agency dispatch on the 17th.]

(Nanjing) Luo Wengan will be tasked with inspecting Xinjiang. Reporters have learned that he will depart within a week after the order from the National Government is issued. Those traveling with him include Lin Donghai, Counsellor of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, Yu Zhiang, Secretary, and Feng Youzhen, Secretary of the Ministry of Justice, totaling seven or eight people. The first group will travel by plane first. Luo and the second group will enter Xinjiang via land routes through Henan, Shaanxi, and Gansu, inspecting the judicial plans of various provinces, transferring prisoners to build roads, and developing transportation in the Northwest. After arriving in Xinjiang, he will visit important cities and towns in the Xinjiang border area, which is expected to take about four or five months. Transportation from Shaanxi and Gansu to Xinjiang is of utmost political importance, so Luo is determined to find a way to open it up. Although there are mountains and rivers obstructing the way from Tongguan, Xi'an, Lanzhou, Suzhou, Hami to Dihua, it is all accessible by automobiles. Therefore, Luo has purchased automobiles in Shanghai, making full preparations. After on-site inspections, he will immediately begin preparations to move young prisoners to build roads and cultivate land. The outline of the measures for the prisoner relocation and cultivation plan, consisting of fourteen articles, has long been drafted. [This is according to a Central News Agency dispatch on the 17th.]

(Nanjing) The Central Government dispatched Foreign Minister Luo Wengan to inspect Xinjiang and other provinces like Henan, Shaanxi, and Gansu. Luo has scheduled his departure before the 25th. The Ministry of Foreign Affairs has dispatched Counsellor Lin Chunxian and Secretary Yu Baoxuan, while the Ministry of Judicial Administration has dispatched Secretary Feng Nanzhen and Section Chief Liu Yinglin to accompany him on the inspection. During the inspection period, the duties of the Foreign Minister will be temporarily assumed by Wang, and the duties of the Minister of Justice will be handled on behalf of him by Zheng Tianxi. The Central Political Council approved this on the 16th, and the Executive Yuan submitted it to the National Government on the 17th for formal issuance and appointment. A clear order will be issued immediately. A reporter recently met with Luo, who provided detailed information about his aspirations for this trip. He mentioned that the actual situation in the Northwest frontier awaits investigation. He, holding positions in both the Ministry of Foreign Affairs and the Ministry of Justice, deeply feels that the current judicial situation in Henan, Shaanxi, Gansu, and Xinjiang, as well as the Sino-Soviet trade relations in the Xinjiang border area, need inspection and rectification. He will travel from Tianjin-Pukou Railway to Longhai Railway, passing through Kaifeng, Lanfeng, Zhengzhou, Luoyang, Tongguan, and other places, with stops at each location. He has also prepared long-distance automobiles to go to Xi'an and Lanzhou. He plans to inspect the three provinces of Henan, Shaanxi, and Gansu for about two months, and then spend two months in the north and south of the Tianshan Mountains in Xinjiang, for a total of about four months. Tents and dry rations will be self-prepared. Shao Lizi and Zhu Shaoliang have both sent telegrams saying that they will send teams to escort him through the areas he passes. The total journey is 8,000 miles. In today's chaotic judicial system, prisons everywhere are poorly equipped and overcrowded with criminals. Although the government has recently issued an order to reduce sentences, it is not a fundamental solution. What I want to solve on this trip are: (1) to investigate the actual situation of the courts' implementation of criminal law; (2) to properly plan livelihood plans such as relocating criminals to build roads and self-reform measures. The former will serve as the basis for revising the criminal law, and the latter is an important plan for rectifying the current judicial system. He will discuss practical strategies with local authorities and court officials. Xinjiang is adjacent to Russia, and the trade relationship has never been completely cut off. The former Xinjiang authorities signed a partial trade agreement with Russia. He will bring a draft of this agreement and assess the actual situation, so that when a formal Sino-Soviet trade treaty is signed, the special relationship of the border area will be fully understood. [This is according to a special dispatch on the 17th.]

Soviet Pravda Extensively Discusses the Xinjiang Situation 28

Imperialists Conduct Conspiracy

Using Xinjiang as an Anti-Soviet Battlefield

Muslim Rebellion Instigated by the Japanese

(Moscow) Today, Pravda, in an editorial extensively discussing the recent situation in Xinjiang, pointed out that the western provinces of China have become the stage for a grand conspiracy by British and Japanese imperialists. It stated that imperialists are mobilizing and preparing to realize their grand plan of conquering the entire Central Asia and transforming the entire region into a battlefield for anti-Russian policies. The newspaper stated, "Xinjiang has long been noticed by imperialists (primarily Britain), because the province is a most important link in their policy of controlling Asia. If British imperialism occupies Xinjiang, it will surely be able to realize its plan for Central Asia, in which the forcible seizure of the Soviet Republics of Central Asia occupies an important position. Britain's plan to create a Greater Tibet includes not only Tibet but also Xinjiang, Sichuan, and other parts of China. At the same time, Japanese imperialists are planning to create a Greater Manchuria Kingdom, whose territory will include Manchuria, Inner and Outer Mongolia, Tibet, Sichuan, Shanxi, Gansu, and Xinjiang. The recent Muslim rebellion in Xinjiang, led by General Ma Zhongying, was actually instigated by the Japanese. These Japanese are taking advantage of the oppression of the masses by the Han authorities, the friction between various feudal groups, and the hatred within the ethnic groups to reap benefits. However, representatives of all ethnic groups in Xinjiang oppose Ma's plan to establish an independent country, and the Japanese imperialists in this plan are extremely eager to make the exiled Turkish Prince Abdul Kerim the head of the independent state." The newspaper continued, stating that the actions of rebels in the Kashgar area of Xinjiang to seize power are becoming increasingly tense, while the guidance of the British in this rebellion movement is extraordinarily active. Although Ma Zhongying's forces in northern Xinjiang have been defeated, there are still many remnants of the rebel forces. These armed forces under the direction of the Japanese are led by Turkish officers, who can still be used in a new war when establishing a Pan-Islamic independent state. Pravda concluded, stating, "The conspiracy of the imperialists in Xinjiang is now proceeding vigorously. The imperialists are preparing their strength to realize their grand plan of subjugating Central Asia, and the British and Japanese imperialists are using the area as a battlefield for anti-Soviet policies." [This is according to a TASS dispatch on the 16th.]

Wang Yingyu Discusses Emergency Measures for Governing the Yellow River 35

(Nanjing) Xu Xinwu, a member of the Yellow River Conservancy Commission, has been appointed to preside over the dikes of the lower reaches of the Yellow River. He is scheduled to go to Zhenjiang on the 18th to negotiate measures with the Jiangsu Provincial Government, and then proceed to northern Jiangsu and the provinces of Hebei, Shandong, and Henan to jointly prepare for the Yellow River Conservancy Commission. Wang Yingyu, the vice chairman, returned to Nanjing from Lushan on the 17th to follow the Central Government's planning for governing the Yellow River. According to him, the dikes along the Yellow River have been in disrepair for many years, and the effectiveness of the existing facilities is decreasing day by day. Due to economic constraints and the lack of time, comprehensive plans for fundamental solutions cannot be carried out. Therefore, the Commission plans to use temporary measures to prevent major disasters, namely: 1. Diverting the Tao River into the Wei River to reduce the amount of sand in the ocean, while the silt in the Hetao region can flow into Ningxia with the water. 2. Expediting the construction of smoke stone dikes from Mengjin to Gubaizui and water containment projects from Mengjin to Dongming. 3. Dredging the river mouth dikes below Lijin. 4. Disposing of a large amount of huge stones to reinforce the Yellow River Railway Bridge. 5. Utilizing the army and workers for construction. However, this project requires a huge amount of funding and must wait until Minister Song returns to the country to find ways to plan and implement it. Recently, it has been necessary to rely on the concerted efforts of the four provinces of Hebei, Shandong, Henan, and Jiangsu to jointly plan and prevent dredging and other matters. It would be fortunate if the disaster area could be kept from becoming too large and the disaster situation could be kept from becoming too severe. [This is according to a special dispatch on the 17th.]

Song Zheyuan Sends a Telegram Requesting Aid for the Disaster in Chahar 36

Zhangjiakou - Song Zheyuan's telegram states, "To all newspaper offices, since the loss of Rehe, Chahar Province has become the first line of national defense. Troops defending against aggression are stationed everywhere, and defeated soldiers and bandits have retreated into Chahar. The burden of providing supplies is heavy. When Dolon fell, the anti-Japanese army rose up. The land is small and the number of soldiers is large. All means of exploitation have been used, and all vehicles and livestock have been requisitioned. The people have fled, displaced and in dire straits. The vitality of the region has been greatly damaged. Now that the military affairs have come to an end and order is gradually being restored, the villages in the northern counties of Kou have become ruins and are now places with land but no people. The counties along the railway have been frequently requisitioned, and grain and fodder have been exhausted. Bandits are everywhere, and the people have no means of livelihood. This originally poor border region has experienced an unprecedented catastrophe. Externally, the strong enemy has not yet been subdued, and internally, the starving are everywhere. The disaster situation is extremely severe and requires urgent rescue. Zheyuan is responsible for comforting and providing relief but lacks the ability to do so. Seeing this scene of devastation, my heart is burning with anxiety. In addition to sending telegrams to President Wang and Chairman Chiang, and the North China War Zone Relief Committee, requesting them to send personnel to Chahar to investigate the disaster and provide relief, I beg you to show great compassion, help us through this difficult time, and make a collective appeal to rescue the dying remnants. I will sincerely pray for your blessings. Song Zheyuan, stamped." [This is according to a special dispatch on the 17th.]

Ministries of Interior and Justice Convene a Fingerprint Conference 46

(Nanjing) The Ministries of Interior and Justice have scheduled a fingerprint conference in Nanjing on November 1st. The fingerprint methods used by police and judicial agencies in various parts of our country, modeled after the German and French fingerprint styles, are quite inconsistent. The Ministry of Interior conference last year had a proposal to unify fingerprints, so this meeting is being convened. Participants include the Ministry of Interior, the Ministry of Justice, public security agencies in provinces and cities across the country, and courts. Representatives will be nominated, bringing proposals to Nanjing to attend the meeting. The provinces and cities will also instruct the public security agencies of counties and towns under their jurisdiction, and the higher courts of each province will instruct the local courts to follow the unified methods if they have already used them, and to quickly comply if they have not yet used them, to facilitate investigation work. The Ministry of Interior will prepare to establish a fingerprint school next year. [This is according to a special dispatch on the 17th.]

Iraqi Incident 68

Gu'er People Massacre the Innocent

British Prime Minister Seeks Friendly Advice

Reuters dispatch from London, 17th: The seriousness of the recent Assyrian incident in Iraq can be seen from the British government's formal protest and the British ambassador's hasty return to Iraq. According to sources in London, 1,500 Assyrians near Mosul, north of the Tigris River, rebelled under the leadership of Mahim Meng. The Iraqi army went to suppress the rebellion, killing 500 Assyrians, but only 90 of those killed were actual rebels. The rest were civilians living in nearby villages. In one village, 315 innocent people were killed. It is believed that the Gu'er people in the Iraqi army, who have always been hostile to the Assyrians, used the insignificant rebellion as an excuse to massacre the innocent. The commander of the northern Iraqi region, Beike'er, is also known for his hatred of the Assyrians. However, Iraq denies the incident, saying that there has been no fighting since the rebels surrendered their weapons on August 11. King Faisal of Iraq has suspended his travels and will return to the country within days.

Reuters dispatch from London, 17th: British Prime Minister MacDonald, who was vacationing in the countryside, has suddenly returned here. It is said that this is due to the massacre of hundreds of Assyrian Christians in Iraq. Foreign Secretary Simon is on sick leave, and the Prime Minister has agreed to act as Foreign Secretary in his absence. That is why he urgently returned to London. Official circles here are deeply anxious about the news of the massacre of over 300 people and King Faisal of Iraq's planned trip abroad. Although Britain is no longer the trustee of Iraq, and therefore not practically responsible, Iraq's independence was proposed by Britain. Now that the situation is deteriorating, some powers will again argue that Iraq does not yet have the qualifications of a nation. The Assyrians fought alongside the Allies in Mesopotamia during the European War and are now being massacred, which may provoke public outrage among the Allied countries. The Iraqi army in the north has indeed been subjected to considerable provocation, but the current situation is largely due to King Faisal's poor management. If King Faisal had a firm hand and punished those responsible, especially the northern army commander Peizhi'er, who is friendly to Turkey, the situation could be salvaged. It is expected that British Prime Minister MacDonald will do his best to advise King Faisal, in a friendly diplomatic manner, not to leave the country at present and to take a firm stance.

Merger of Three Japanese Banks 69

Sanwa Bank Emerges

Japan United News dispatch from Osaka, 17th: The merger of Yamaguchi, Konoike, and Thirty-Fourth banks has been realized. The conditions are as follows: (1) The rights and obligations of the three banks are, in principle, equal, but initially, Konoike Bank will hold two shares, and Yamaguchi and Thirty-Fourth banks will each hold one share. (2) The capital after the merger will be 107.2 million yen. (3) The name of the three banks after the merger will be Sanwa Bank. (4) The general manager of the new bank will be decided by the president of the Bank of Japan. The Ministry of Finance authorities issued a statement regarding the merger of the three banks, saying that the three banks automatically implemented the merger to promote rational management. The three banks, in view of the economic situation, organized a strong new bank to prepare for future activities, which is very gratifying. The integration of banks with strong individual characteristics into a common new bank is of great significance. It is said that the formal signing will be implemented in November.

For several years since the German Revolution, foreign tourists in Germany have made bad criticisms of German customs. The authorities have decided to eliminate this stain. Now, foreign tourists in Germany no longer make these comments. The practice of soliciting in the streets has been banned. The bad women have all been sent to factories. In the future, any man who sets foot in these places will be punished along with the owner.

Communication Established Between Anyuan and Xunwu 73

Guangzhou correspondence: After suffering setbacks in Liancheng, the Communist bandits in western Fujian, the 19th Route Army has gathered heavy troops and is advancing towards Changting. At the same time, it informed the Southern Route Bandit Suppression Army on the Guangdong-Jiangxi border to advance in different directions to divide the bandit forces. Recently, the Second Column of the Southern Route Bandit Suppression Army, the Huang Renhuan Division, has mobilized four regiments to guard Shanghang and another three regiments to deploy in Wuping. At the same time, the Seventh and Eighth Divisions also advanced from Xunwu. The Second Independent Division, Zhang Ruigui's unit, took over defenses in the Jiaoling and Pingyuan areas. The Fifth Division of the Second Army, Zhang Da's unit, also advanced to Xingning for deployment. The units of the First Column in southern Jiangxi, after arriving near Anyuan recently, have not been able to establish contact with the Seventh and Eighth Divisions of the Second Column in Xunwu because several bandit strongholds north of Anyuan have not been captured. Currently, the Anyuan garrison, Zhang Meixin and Wang Zanbin's divisions, are conducting a search and suppression operation towards Zun Sanwei, and have successively broken through twelve bandit strongholds in the area. The remaining two bandit strongholds have been under siege for more than a month, but without success. Recently, the Third Air Force Team, led by Tao Zuode, has been transferred to Longnan, and sends planes with bombs to bomb the bandit strongholds every day. The troops are also fiercely besieging. By the 8th of this month, more than 800 bandits broke through and fled due to the destruction of their defenses and the exhaustion of their food. They were intercepted by government troops along the way, suffering more than 100 casualties. The remnant bandits fled to Huichang via Datangxu and Shangxiaping. On the same day, Wang Shi's Zhou Yuan Regiment occupied one of the last strongholds of the Communist bandits, while Zhang Shi's Kong Regiment is now stationed in Dongshixu, Li Regiment is stationed in Banshixu, Chen Regiment is stationed in Gangtouzhai, and Jiang Regiment is stationed in Longtou. Currently, the northeast and northwest of Anyuan have been solidified by the deployment of Zhang and Wang's divisions. In the future, the First and Second Columns of the Southern Route Bandit Suppression Army will have established considerable contact between Anyuan and Xunwu. The situation in the Huichang bandit lair in eastern Jiangxi is becoming increasingly dangerous. It is expected that the Jiangxi bandits will not dare to invade south in the short term, and may implement a plan to flee north and invade west. According to a telegram from Chen Cheng of the Central Bandit Suppression Army yesterday, more than 1,000 Red Bandits suddenly attacked Fengcheng, three miles from Fuzhou, on the 5th of this month. They were armed with sharp weapons and were quite rampant. The defending forces near Fengcheng were weak and had to temporarily retreat to the city. The rice fields outside the city have all been looted by the bandits. Chen Cheng has deployed a certain unit to prepare to encircle and suppress the bandit forces. (August 13)

Yellow River Overflow in Western Shandong 74

The Water Level of the North Canal Rises Sharply

Jinan Correspondence: The Yellow River in Hebei and Henan has flooded western Shandong. Heze and Cao County have already seen water, and it is now flowing everywhere. Today (14th), the water has reached Gaodigou in Heze County and is continuing to overflow eastward. The water that breached Shitou Zhuang on the north bank of Changyuan has reached Zhangqingying, 18 li from Fan County, today (15th). The water flows downstream along the Dike South Jiahe ditch, and has not overflowed the banks. It is 1.67 meters deep and 40-50 meters wide. The provincial government has sent Councilor Zhang Shouqian and Deputy Director Wang Shaochang of the Zouping Rural Construction Institute to Caozhou to assist in prevention and investigate the disaster to provide a basis for relief. As for the North Canal (Wei River) in northern Shandong, the water level has risen sharply due to continuous heavy rains. According to a telegram from Yao Xintian, a technician sent by the Department of Construction to Dezhou, and Li Shude, the magistrate of De County, the water level has exceeded the highest flood level by one foot and three inches, and the water depth is one zhang and four chi and eight cun, which is two chi and two cun from the top of the dike. According to a telegram from Zhen Guangyuan, the magistrate of Wucheng County, the river water is continuing to rise. The water level is 30.248. The old brick of the Qiliting Gray Dam has collapsed, and the Sanlikou Gray Dam is also overflowing by three to four inches. The magistrate is supervising the civilians to rush to repair it. The Department of Construction has ordered all counties along the river to step up precautions to prevent the floods in western Shandong from spreading to northern Shandong. The telegrams from Wucheng and De counties are recorded below. (1) Telegram from Wucheng: Addressed to Zhang Jun, Director of the Department of Construction. We have reported the situation of the rising and falling water level of the canal in this county by telegram. Now we have checked the canal water level. From 6:00 p.m. on August 12th to 2:00 p.m. on the 13th, it has risen by about three cun and three fen. The current water level is 30.248, which is only three cun away from the highest flood level in recent years. There have been heavy rains every night for the past three days, and the water level has been rising every day. The old brick in front of Qiliting has collapsed, and the gray dam has been overflowing for three to four inches since that day. The magistrate has personally led civilians to add soil and repair the dam by more than two chi. There are no other dangerous signs in other places. In addition to working with Li Cishan, a technician from the Department of Construction, and Liu Shuxiang, a water conservancy commissioner, to supervise the civilians and police day and night to do their best to protect various dangerous projects to prevent unforeseen circumstances, we hereby report to you for verification. Zhen Guangyuan, Magistrate of Wucheng County, bows to you. (2) Telegram from De County: (1) Addressed to Zhang Jun, Director of the Department of Construction. The canal water has been rising again since the 11th, rising sharply by six chi and eight cun in three days. The current water level has reached 15 chi and 7 cun, which has exceeded the highest flood level by one chi and two cun. It is still rising. In addition to paying attention to protection, we hereby report to you. Yao Xintian bows to you. (2) (Title omitted) On August 13th, the canal in De County was 24 chi and 8 cun deep, which is two chi and five cun higher than yesterday, and two chi and two cun from the top of the dike. In addition to the magistrate continuing to supervise the civilians to actively protect it, we hereby report to you. (August 15)

Guangdong Province Restrains Women's Clothing 75

Department of Finance Orders Female Staff to Respect Themselves

Bureau of Social Affairs Prohibits Bare Feet and Short Skirts

Guangzhou correspondence: District Fangpu, special commissioner of finance and director of the Department of Finance, recently issued a notice on the 10th to the female staff of the department, admonishing them for continuously improving their clothing and losing their solemnity. The notice stated, "It is hereby noted that women serving in government agencies are government employees. Regarding their appearance and clothing, they should have a solemn appearance. Although there are no regulations for female staff uniforms, they should still be simple and unadorned. However, it has recently been found that some female staff in the department cannot avoid being vulgar and pursue fashion, decorating their hair and nails, applying powder and rouge, and wearing green and red clothes to compete with each other, which degrades their personality and loses their solemnity. It is urgent to correct this in order to save the declining habits. You are hereby instructed to follow this notice. In the future, you must refrain from being extravagant, wash off your makeup, and wear homespun clothes. Do not deliberately violate this, lest you be investigated. This is of utmost importance."

Zhang Yuanfeng, director of the Guangzhou Bureau of Social Affairs, also stated that licentious appearance leads to immorality, and there has long been a ban on it. Strange and enchanting clothing is of great concern to public morals. Moreover, many women in the city often go barefoot, and the cicada gauze and brightly colored clothes they wear are colorful, and the lower skirts are also shortened, causing passersby to stare. It is inevitable that young people with unstable blood will be involved in immoral thoughts. In order to rectify public morals and save declining customs, they should be banned. Therefore, it is now planned to standardize things so that women know what to follow. All strange clothing is prohibited. It is said that the plan has been completed and will be implemented soon. (August 13)

Shaanxi Province Floods Worsen 76

Affected Area Reaches More Than Thirty Counties

Disaster Is Unusually Severe, Unseen in a Century

Xi'an correspondence: Since 1928, Shaanxi Province has been plagued by droughts. People in various counties have been displaced, and the fields in rural areas have been barren and desolate. The tragedy of the disaster is unbearable to hear. Since the beginning of summer this year, there has been frost and hail, affecting sixty to seventy counties. After the summer harvest, the harvest throughout the province has been poor. Most of the victims have nothing to live on. Recently, heavy rains have continued to fall, causing mountain torrents and rivers to swell. Countless houses have been washed away, and countless people and livestock have been washed away. In Qiaodi Town, Jingyang alone, more than 1,000 corpses have been found. Near Louti Village in northeastern Sanyuan, nearly four to five thousand bodies have recently been found, which is truly shocking. After the heavy rains, telegrams and letters from various counties reporting to the government and requesting relief came one after another.

A Glimpse of the Disaster 77

The counties affected by the floods include Chang'an, Sanyuan, Xianyang, Jingyang, Weinan, Huayin, Hua County, Dali, Pucheng, Fuping, Fufeng, Lantian, Chaoyi, Baoji, Chunhua, Wugong, Pingmin, Gaoling, Hu County, Changwu, Yichuan, Shiquan, Lin County, Ziyang, Yulin, Mizhi, Luochuan, Fugu, Jingbian, Jia County, and other thirty-odd counties. Among them, the areas around Zhongnan Mountain and the mountains north of the Wei River are the most severely affected. It is reported that during the torrential rains, the rivers flowing down the mountains, as well as the Chan River, Ba River, Li River, Jue River, and Zao River, all swelled suddenly. In addition, mountain torrents from the valleys broke out, which were extremely fierce. As a result, houses in places such as Kuyukou, Dayukou, Xiaoyukou, and Tangyukou were completely washed away. Property and belongings could not be moved in time. Residents and passing travelers were unable to escape and drowned. According to a preliminary investigation, no fewer than 10,000 residents have drowned. From Yukou to Gaoqiao, a distance of seventy li, all the fields along the river were washed away, totaling more than a thousand qing. The corpses of residents who were washed away by the water, with missing hands and feet, were everywhere along the river. They were all washed to the confluence of the Chan and Ba rivers and eventually floated on the beach along the river. The situation was so terrible that people could not bear to look at it. Lu Yu Yan, south of the city, is a historically famous levee. There is a saying, "If the Lu Yu Yan is breached, Chang'an will disappear." Its importance is evident. This time, it was breached, causing the area outside the south gate of the provincial capital to become a vast ocean. The water only receded after more than ten days. In the Weibei area, the water volume of the Qing and Zhuo rivers in Sanyuan suddenly rose to eight or nine zhang. The villages and houses along the river were all washed away, and hundreds of men and women drowned. No fewer than a thousand qing of farmland were washed away. In Jingyang, the Zhiyu and Qingyu rivers and the areas along the rivers have all become swamps. Even the famous and largest water conservancy project, the Jinghui Canal, was damaged by the raging water. According to a report from the Shaanxi Water Conservancy Bureau, the bridges and culverts of each main canal could not discharge the water in time due to the heavy rain. The most severely damaged was the Minsheng Bridge on the main canal, which was completely washed away, leaving only the bridge holes. A section of the stone bridge on the North Canal and more than ten places on the embankments of the main canal were breached. Several places downstream of the Baofeng Temple on the South Canal were washed away, and farmland was also irrigated in places with high canal bottoms. The bureau has urgently assessed the bridges and culverts and will implement emergency earthwork as soon as possible to avoid further damage. During this mountain torrent, the residents along the Shichuan River in the territory of Fuping Linzhang suffered particularly severely. South of Fuping, more than 500 homes have been washed away below Xiangqiao, and no less than a thousand qing of farmland has been submerged. According to local farmers, this flood is rare in a century. In the Wei River Basin, except for Yangping Town in Baoji, which was affected by the rising river water and washed away two-thirds of the town's streets and more than ten large and small villages, the loss was relatively small because there were few residents along the coast. Therefore, only a few beaches were flooded. In the Yellow River Basin, the number of houses and fields washed away along the river is even more countless, especially in Pingmin and Chaoyi. It is said that when the Pingmin River rose sharply, most of the West Gate Tower, temples, and houses collapsed. The area from the east gate of the city to Yongji County in Shanxi Province became like a river, which shows the magnitude of the water. The area within the territory of Chaoyi County, east to west for twenty to thirty li, has become a vast ocean. The situation is even worse. The areas affected by the floods in the counties of northern Shaanxi are also very large. However, the reports received are not detailed. The above is only a description of the most severely affected areas. In other counties such as Wugong, Shiquan, and Changwu, there is almost no way to investigate the houses and fields washed away and the people and livestock drowned. Shaanxi Province, which has always been known as a drought-prone area, has actually developed into such a strange disaster.

Jiang Song

Office of Funds and Property Cables Request to Exempt Additional Grain Tribute 78

The grain tribute in Jiangsu Province is the heaviest in the country. During the era when Sun Chuanfang governed Jiangsu, an additional two yuan per stone of winter tribute was levied, to be deducted in the following year. However, year after year, not only has it not been returned, but it has also been levied continuously. The people have been burdened for three years. The Office of Funds and Property of this county previously submitted a request for exemption, and received a reply limiting it to one year. Therefore, they advised them to endure the pain and complete the payment. Recently, there has been talk of continuing to request the Ministry of Finance to continue the additional levy. The director of the Office of Funds and Property, Li Zuhua, believes that the rice price has fallen sharply this year, all industries are declining, and the economic situation in rural society is showing decline. It is already on the verge of bankruptcy, which shows that the people are poor and the wealth is exhausted. If the additional levy is continued, the people will find it difficult to bear the burden. He sent a telegram to the Ministry of Finance, Minister Song, and Provincial Chairman Gu today (17th), urging them to approve the cancellation of the proposal to continue the additional levy of the winter tribute in order to relieve the people of Jiangsu.

Suzhou 79

Youth Commits Suicide in Suzhou, Suspicious

On the 13th, a young man in a western suit, who looked handsome, came to the Dadong Hotel outside Yanmen. He wrote his name as Huang Wen, a native of Guangdong, 25 years old, studying at Fudan University in Shanghai. He opened room 213. After the guest lived in the room, he never went out, and no one came to visit. The tea attendant, Wang Liansheng, was suspicious, so he paid attention. He then saw him writing several letters quickly and going to the post office to mail them himself. One of them was discovered by Wang to be addressed to Ms. Lu Fuzhen, No. 99 Shiquan Street, Suzhou City, with the words "Dragon Seal" written below. He only went out once on the evening of the 16th. After returning, he ordered the tea attendant to buy ten packs of white tin. He then lay down after a moment of enjoying the cool air. On the morning of the 17th, Wang Liansheng saw that he had not gotten up. When he went to check again at noon, he saw that he was already unconscious. He immediately reported to the Second Division of the Public Security Bureau and sent the guest to the hospital. However, just as he was being carried to the back door, a long-distance call suddenly came from the Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau, saying that there was a person named Huang Wen who had come to commit suicide and asking them to pay attention. The guest was carried to the nearby Suyong Hospital, where Dr. Gu Suyong urgently rescued him. It was found that he had taken sleeping pills. At 5:00 p.m., he was still unconscious. However, Dr. Gu discovered that the words "Long Xun" were written on the reverse side of the young man's western suit pants. Combined with the words "Dragon Seal" on the letter to Shiquan Street, it can be determined that his real name is Long Xun. Afterwards, two waste envelopes were found in the spittoon in the guest's room, both addressed to Director Wen of the Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau for opening. There were also two suicide notes, one to the reporter and one to the Dadong Hotel. After the incident, it caused a stir in society. The reporter telegraphed Officer Tang of the Second Division of the Public Security Bureau, and learned that No. 99 Shiquan Street was the residence of a Sichuan widow, Ms. Lu Min. The relationship with the suicide victim, and whether Long's letter had been delivered, is still under investigation. The original text of the letter left to Dadong Hotel was, "To the owner of this hotel, I am sorry to use your hotel as a place to kill myself. I know this is not right, so I am very sorry. But I do not owe any rent, and I have prepared 20 yuan (in the silver bag) to compensate you for all your losses, which I think will not be a big problem. Please keep my body here temporarily, and someone from Shanghai will take care of everything." The letter to the newspaper office said, "Mr. Reporter, I am not heartbroken, nor am I unemployed, nor am I under economic pressure, nor is it due to any disputes. People's personalities are different, and their viewpoints are also different. My passive suicide is a very different idea from others. As for the reason, it is still up to the reader to study. How can I not say it? Please do not exaggerate the matter in the newspaper."

Another long-distance telephone message said that the young man in a western suit who committed suicide with sleeping pills at Dadong was named Long Daozhen, a native of Qiongzhou Prefecture, Guangdong Province, and a relative of Director Wen. He was formerly a patrol officer in the Second District of Shanghai and is now transferred to the General Bureau as a patrol officer. His parents are both in his hometown, and he was engaged since childhood. The reason for his suicide this time was dissatisfaction with the marriage. At 6:00 p.m., the Shanghai Public Security Bureau had sent Long He, a member of the First Section, and Wen Dake, the chief inspector of the police brigade, to Suzhou. His girlfriend, Lu Fuzhen, also called the hospital to inquire about the truth. It was found that Lu was 21 years old and a famous socialite in Suzhou. She went to the capital to work this spring and now lives at No. 99 Shiquan Street, Suzhou.

Sun Apan Kills Adulterer with a Knife 80

Sun Apan, near Le Hu on Hulong Street, is a local vagrant. Yesterday afternoon, he returned home from outside and went straight into his mother's room. He unexpectedly saw a man, whose name he did not know, sitting on the edge of the bed in his mother's room, talking to his mother in a soft voice. He believed that he must be his mother's lover and immediately drove him away. However, his mother protected him, so Sun Apan became enraged and took a knife, slashing the man's neck fiercely. At that time, the skin broke and blood flowed, but the man was timid and did not dare to fight back. He fled outwards with his injury. Sun Apan wanted to chase after him, but was held back by his mother, so he had to let him escape. The incident was known to the police district in charge and is currently under investigation.

Imminent Danger to the Chongming City Southern Seawall 81

Chongming is located at the mouth of the Yangtze River, surrounded by the sea, and is the throat of the Yangtze River, a strategically important place for coastal defense. Since its establishment as a county in the Song Dynasty, due to the erosion of the river water, the land has been constantly collapsing and expanding, and the county seat has been moved five times. In the twenty-sixth year of the Guangxu reign of the Qing Dynasty, the local people successively petitioned the government to build a stone seawall more than a thousand feet long on the south side of the city, and the people donated 5,000 mu of sandy fields, which were named "Seawall Public Fields," as funds for the annual repair of the seawall. Over the years, the seawall has been repaired and has remained safe and sound. In the seventeenth year of the Republic of China, the outer sand area of the county was separated for governance (now Qidong). As a result, all public properties were divided item by item. Although the plan was decided, it has not yet been implemented. Last year, people from Chongming and Qidong counties requested joint governance, but the plan was shelved by the provincial government. Recently, the seawall project on the south side of the county seat has been in extreme danger. The Department of Construction sent a supervising engineer to measure the site. In front of the Qinglong Dam, the whirlpool depth reached 45 meters and the width was nearly one mile. More than 20 feet of the stone slope have collapsed. It is estimated that the repair project will cost more than 100,000 yuan. People are panicked. The county Kuomintang first telegraphed the province to petition for relief. The county farmers' association and other organizations, as well as local gentry such as Wang Qingmu and Zhu Songhan, jointly submitted a petition to the province to request the issuance of overdue subsidies and the public rents of the seawall occupied by Qidong County in order to carry out emergency repairs. They also sent Cheng Tiyun, a member of the county executive committee, and Tao Zhu, the director of the property department, to the province to petition the provincial government and the finance department. During the high tide of this month, more than three feet of the stone slope collapsed again, and the danger is extreme. If funds are not raised for repairs, the consequences will be unimaginable.

Gao Yihan of Wuxi Arrives in Wuxi for Inspection 82

Gao Yihan, a member of the Control Yuan of the National Government, arrived in Wuxi by train from Suzhou at 12:40 PM on the 16th, accompanied by his secretary Huang Renzhong and two servants. He stayed in rooms 24 and 25 of the Railway Hotel. Zhou Erkai, the chief prosecutor of the county court, Yan Shenyu, the county magistrate, and Ye Dezhen, the secretary, went to the hotel to pay their respects after receiving the news. Mr. Gao inquired in detail about the local political situation. Yesterday morning, at 8:00 AM, he went to the county government, the county court, the prison administration, the detention center, the police station, and the education bureau for inspection. The results were satisfactory. According to Mr. Gao's statement to reporters, the purpose of this trip is to inspect the public sentiment in Jiangsu Province and the dike construction in Jiangbei, and the Songbao seawall project, which have recently been inspected. As for the impeachment case of Zhao Qi, the authorities have their own handling methods. There is no news about the reorganization of the Jiangsu Provincial Government. When Mr. Gao inspected the county government, he was received by County Magistrate Yan, who led him to the county magistrate's office. After a brief exchange of greetings, Mr. Gao immediately inquired about the administrative situation of Wuxi County, asking about the situation of public security, autonomy, land tax, and education. He also inquired about the general situation of the Wanye Guidance Center. County Magistrate Yan gave him a detailed account one by one. Mr. Gao also paid close attention to the prison issue. Prisons in various counties are often overcrowded. He inquired into the reasons, whether it was due to the delay in trying cases or the small size of the prison buildings. Now Mr. Gao is going to various counties for on-the-spot inspections to find out the truth. Mr. Gao is scheduled to leave Wuxi for Nanjing at 12:00 PM today (the 18th).

Butchers in Changzhou Strike Over Slaughter Tax 83

The slaughter tax in Wu County has always been contracted by Liu Hesheng. Butchers have repeatedly accused him of illegally overcharging. Recently, the annual term has expired, and Liu Hesheng still contracted the tax for 29,000 yuan and issued a notice to collect it. Upon hearing the news, the butchers sent representatives to the county government and the county Kuomintang on the afternoon of the 16th to request relief. At that time, they advised the merchants to directly ask the Education Funding Management Office for instructions on how to handle the matter and wait quietly for a solution. The butchers' representatives, failing to obtain a satisfactory result, immediately convened a general meeting of all members of the Meat Industry Association at 5:00 PM and unanimously decided to temporarily stop slaughtering pigs. More than 20 members have all suspended business, and representatives have been sent to the Jiangsu Provincial Education Funding Management Office to petition for the removal of Liu Hesheng. They must wait for instructions before resuming business. Therefore, since the 17th, except for those who are related to the slaughter tax, who continue to operate as usual, all others have unanimously suspended business.

Nanjing Artist Wu Nanyu Arrives in Nanjing 84

Mr. Wu Nanyu from Beiping is proficient in seal engraving, calligraphy, and painting, especially iron-point calligraphy. He can carve more than 6,000 characters in a square inch of ivory, as fine as hair, exquisitely and magically. The paintings he carves are extremely small, but mountains, rivers, trees, figures, boats, pavilions, bridges, and everything else are all complete, just like the composition of a large painting, a work of supernatural craftsmanship, a unique skill for all ages. In the past two or three years, Mr. Wu has meticulously carved and stored many masterpieces. Now, he has brought a large number of works from Beiping in batches and displayed them in the dining hall of the Central Hotel in Daxing Palace for the people of the capital to appreciate together.

Hangzhou Executes Wang Zhen for Shielding the Smuggling of Red Pills 85

Wang Zhen, the special agent of the 34th Regiment of the Sixth Army and the director of the Hangzhou garrison, colluded with Zhou Lihe, the former clerk of the Sixth Army, to carry a large number of red pills. They were seized in the provincial capital and transferred to the Provincial Security Office for interrogation. According to Wang's confession, the red pills were entrusted to him to be transported to Quzhou. Zhou Lihe denied the accusation of carrying red pills, claiming that he was going to the front line in Jiangxi with Wang Zhen. However, according to Wang's confession, they were indeed transporting them together. It was found that Wang Zhen, as an active duty military officer, dared to collude with Zhou Lihe to shield the smuggling of red pills, which was a serious crime. According to the Criminal Law of the Army, Navy, and Air Force and the regulations of this province on eliminating drugs, he was sentenced to death. With the approval of Chairman Chiang Kai-shek, the Provincial Security Office sent personnel to the military prison yesterday (the 17th) at 8:00 AM to bring out Wang Zhen and Zhou Lihe, verify their identities, and tie them to the open space of the first pier in Jianggan for execution by firing squad.

American Far East Trade 93

Still Holds Leading Position

The "Ta Mei Wan Bao" (Greater America Evening News) said that the trade of the United States in China and the Far East can still be the best compared to other countries, and it has been in a leading position in import and export trade for three years. According to Chinese customs and other statistics, in the first six months of this year, 20.3 percent of China's imports came from the United States, and 18.51 percent of its exports went to the United States. Japan ranks second, and the United Kingdom ranks third. In recent months, trade between Japan and China has increased sharply, but it is still far behind the United States. Kerosene and its by-products, as well as tobacco, cotton, and timber, are the four elements that contribute to the large amount of American imports. Chinese cotton, eggs, leather, fur, peanuts, raw oil, silk, tea, wool, and antimony are the main exports from China to the United States. However, the benefits of trade after the recent increase in the price of silver have been mostly offset by the inflation of currency and the increase in prices in the United States. According to a report from the US Department of Commerce, in May of this year, the total value of US trade with the Far East was 51,375,000 gold yuan, an increase of 7,858,000 gold yuan compared with 43,517,000 gold yuan in April. Imports accounted for a larger portion of this increase. However, compared with the same period last year, it decreased by 3,643,000 yuan, or about 6.6 percent. Losses in 1933 commercial exports were particularly affected, apparently due to the price drop of certain American goods and oriental raw silk and hemp products. In May 1933, the value of goods exported from the United States to various countries in the Far East was 20,096,000 US dollars, a decrease of nearly 20.5 percent compared to 25,283,000 US dollars in May of the previous year. This loss, although a result of lower prices, is also due to the increase in production of domestic and foreign factories in various countries, so the sales of goods from Europe and the United States have decreased. Exports to Japan alone saw an increase, jumping from 5,883,000 US dollars to 8,676,000 US dollars. Exports to China decreased from 4,545,000 US dollars to 4,217,000 US dollars. Exports to the Philippines decreased from 3,967,000 US dollars to 3,579,000 US dollars. The total value of export trade in May increased by more than 17 percent compared to the same month last year, an increase of 17,194,000 US dollars. The demand for raw cotton, timber, cigarettes, steel, refining, mineral oil, and freight cars is increasing in the East, while tobacco, machinery, automobiles, and electrical equipment are on a downward trend. Exports to Japan in May increased by 29 percent compared to April. The total value of goods exported to China increased from 3,444,000 yuan in April to 4,217,000 yuan in May.

Fang Jianfei is Suddenly Chopped by Thugs with Axes 94

The Shoe Industry Union Issued a Declaration Yesterday

To Petition the Party and Government This Morning to Arrest the Murderers

Xin Sheng She reports that Fang Jianfei, the executive director of the Shanghai Shoe Manufacturing Industry Union, was suddenly attacked by thugs with sharp axes at Ren Zhi Li, North Sichuan Road, at 9:00 PM on the 14th of this month, resulting in serious injuries and disability. The union issued a declaration and decided to petition the party and government agencies this morning.

Thugs Commit Murder The Shoe Manufacturing Industry Union told the Xin Sheng She reporter yesterday that Fang Jianfei, the executive director, is a worker at the Xianghua Shoe Store on Avenue Joffre. At 9:00 PM on the 14th of this month, while passing through Ren Zhi Li on North Sichuan Road, the entrance of the union, he met his colleague Fan Yiqiang. While they were talking on the road, more than ten thugs suddenly appeared, each holding a sharp axe and speaking in a Cantonese accent. Without asking any questions, they chopped at Fang Jianfei, causing both arms to break, and he fell to the ground unconscious. Fan Yiqiang was also affected. The police sent Fang to the Tongren Hospital for treatment. Seeing that their goal had been achieved, the thugs fled without a trace. After Fang was sent to the hospital, the doctor treated him, and his life was saved, but he was disabled. Fang is a worker in leather shoes and serves as the executive director of the union. He has no personal grudges on weekdays. Now that he has been assassinated, it is obvious that there is a background, hoping to disrupt the labor movement and eliminate the union organization. In addition to reporting to the court to severely punish the murderers, the union will submit a petition to the Municipal Party Headquarters and the Social Affairs Bureau on the morning of the 18th, requesting assistance in strictly arresting those who destroy the labor movement.

Union Declaration The Shoe Manufacturing Industry Union issued a declaration yesterday, saying, "To the Central Party Headquarters of the Kuomintang of China, the National Government, the Party Headquarters and Courts of all provinces and cities, and the General Unions of all provinces and cities: Our union's executive director, Mr. Fang Jianfei, was passing through Ren Zhi Li, North Sichuan Road, at 9:00 PM on the 14th of this month when he met his friend Fan Yiqiang and exchanged a few words. Suddenly, more than ten thugs came, with fierce and brutal momentum, and suddenly took out sharp weapons such as knives and axes and chopped at our union's executive director and his friend Fan without asking any questions, causing them to suffer serious injuries. The police sent them to the police station and then to the hospital for treatment. The criminals were all hiding in Qinglu, No. 50, Tong De Li, Wuchang Road. Two murderers were arrested that night by detectives in the residence. The rest were missing. The case is still under trial in the First Special District Court on the 15th and has not yet been adjudicated. Fang Jianfei has always been peaceful and diligent in all union affairs, working hard and constructing in a systematic way, regardless of external affairs, and is deeply admired by his colleagues. The colleagues are extremely angry at the poisoning of this thug. This situation is that the murderer must have other organizations and many followers, with the purpose of trying to disturb the affairs of the association, destroy the labor movement, and assassinate officials. If these reactionary thugs are not eradicated as soon as possible, not only will our association be disturbed, but all organizations and groups in the city will be affected. Therefore, the colleagues unanimously rose up to help Executive Director Fang, so as to avoid the unjust sinking of the snow. We hereby request the principals of various institutions and groups to uphold morality, come forward to assist, be the backing of our association, and eradicate the reactionary thugs to calm the public's anger. It is fortunate for the society, fortunate for the colleagues. In addition to asking the court to severely punish the detained murderers and investigate the remaining accomplices, we are deeply afraid that all sectors of society will not understand the truth, so we hereby declare."

North Sea Steamship Lines Compete in Price Reduction 96

Merchants Have Forgotten the National Crisis

Goods Are Re-loaded onto Japanese Ships

Recently, Japanese steamship lines have been trying to recover and compete with Chinese and British companies for the export cargo from the northern and southern seas. Since this week, steamships traveling between North China and Japan, such as Nisshin, Showa, Daki, and Osaka, have ostensibly followed the regulations for export freight rates, but secretly they have been giving large rebates and indiscriminately reducing freight rates, even reducing the amount by 50 or 60 percent. General merchants, only seeking cheap fees, have re-loaded their goods onto Japanese ships. Therefore, in the past few days, most of the goods shipped from Shanghai to Qingdao and Tianjin have been carried by Japanese ships. Each Japanese steamship export is fully loaded, causing the business of the Chinese and British steamship companies' northern sea routes to be greatly affected.

We await your orders."

Page 12

Zhu Qinglan's Telegraph

Reply to Li Du's Telegraph 99

Provided a detailed explanation of each point in Li's inquiry

Stating that for anything heard, it is hoped to investigate the facts in detail

General Li Du sent another telegram to General Zhu Qinglan on the 14th, inquiring about the use of the anti-Japanese donations and listing various points to clarify the doubts. Zhu replied to Li via telegram yesterday, explaining the facts of each point raised by Li. The two telegrams are recorded separately below:

General Li's Telegram 100

General Li Du sent a fast telegram from Lushan on the 14th to General Zhu Qinglan. The original telegram stated: "Zhu Ziqiao, Shanghai, with respect, I recently received your telegram inquiring about the conversation reported in the newspaper. There was indeed a conversation, but when it was said that you, sir, used 500,000 yuan in donations to open a bank and run a school, it was probably a mishearing by the reporter, resulting in erroneous publication. The receipt of donations of 40,000 to 60,000 yuan refers to those in Beijing, Tianjin, and Shanghai who borrowed the name solely for propaganda, not those who actually resisted the Japanese. It is also not the case that Du's department received and distributed the funds in this way, which is heard with great certainty. However, who presided over this matter, and to whom did the remaining funds go, may not be known to you, sir. In short, there have been many doubts about you, sir, in the past year. Now that I have received your inquiry, I am making a straightforward statement. If you used 500,000 yuan in donations to open a bank in Rehe, you, sir, once said that you were adjusting the financial situation of Rehe Province. It is heard that the central government allocated 400,000 yuan to aid the anti-Japanese armies in the Northeast, and you, sir, sent a batch to Tang Yulin to manufacture 40,000 sets of leather military uniforms and transport them to Rehe, and purchased guns and cannons worth more than 800,000 yuan, storing them in Beiping. The central government issued 6 million rounds of ammunition to supplement the anti-Japanese forces, but it was discovered in Tianjin that your people were privately selling ammunition, and many were arrested and are still in custody. Yang Binlou and Gao Bosheng went to the Northeast on your orders to contact various military units. Since the incident, many people in Beijing, Tianjin, and Shanghai have been borrowing names solely for propaganda and have received more consolation money, while those who actually resist the Japanese have not benefited. I ask, who should be held responsible? The Jilin army launched an uprising in December of the 20th year and continued until January of this year, lasting thirteen months and engaging in more than 120 battles of various sizes. There should have been six regular army brigades, which were later expanded to fourteen brigades, as well as seven detachments of people's volunteer army. Since the fierce battle of Binjiang, each soldier had no more than 200 rounds of ammunition. When they retreated to Muling and the nine counties along the border, which were extremely barren, raising provisions was still difficult, let alone paying salaries. Therefore, from March of last year until they withdrew from the country, a total of ten months, no salaries were paid to the entire officer corps. During the counterattacks on Harbin and Jilin in April and May, the soldiers faced artillery fire, slept in mud, and could not get a full meal all day long. The hardship was heartbreaking. When the Japanese invaders advanced on Boli and Baoqing in September, the late autumn weather was suddenly cold, and the soldiers were all in single clothes and worn shoes, sleeping in the severe frost and light snow at night. Five or six out of ten fell ill due to the cold. At that time, they received a telegram from Beiping saying that you, sir, had promised to raise 200,000 yuan for clothing expenses. After the good news, the entire army was excited. However, only 20,000 yuan was received by late winter, and everyone was disappointed. As a result, they were unable to prepare clothing, and three or four out of ten soldiers did not wear cotton-padded clothes. When the Japanese invaders launched a large-scale offensive at the end of the year, the soldiers were lying in trenches to defend against the enemy in the severe winter cold, and the number of people who froze to death exceeded the casualties in battle. In addition, ammunition was exhausted, and the enemy's armored vehicles advanced, but the soldiers were holding empty guns and were unable to stop them. This allowed the Japanese invaders to gain momentum and eventually withdraw from the country. The main reason was that they were forced into poverty. If you, sir, had fulfilled your previous promise and allocated the full amount, the morale would have been boosted and they would not have suffered such a defeat. The central government allocated ammunition to you, sir, but you did not replenish it. You also made a large number of military uniforms and purchased a large number of guns and cannons. This is why there are rumors that you, sir, were planning your own development. At that time, the troops fighting in the Northeast had no clothing and insufficient ammunition, but you, sir, did not pay attention to this. If you were determined to resist Japan and save the country, you would have provided some assistance to the troops fighting in the Northeast, so that they would not be so impoverished. Yang Junbinlou in Muling and Gao Junbosheng in Dongning claimed to be acting on your orders to contact various military units to form another organization. Anti-Japanese work is a national sacrifice, not a struggle for personal rights. They only knew to save the country and knew nothing else. Therefore, they never understood the intentions of Yang Jun, and the people's consolation donations hoped for by the entire Du's department became silent. At that time, they telegraphed to inquire whether Yang Jun was your representative, and later received a reply acknowledging it. Last winter, the difficulties had reached their extreme. Yang Jun witnessed the situation and repeatedly telegraphed to report the difficult situation, and said that there were more than 3 million yuan in savings in Shanghai, but you, sir, never replied a word. It is believed that you are clear about the real situation of the Jilin army's resistance against Japan. After the incident, many people in Beijing, Tianjin, and Shanghai fabricated facts and fraudulently claimed donations in the name of anti-Japanese propaganda, and even sold ammunition. It is known that you, sir, would certainly not do this. However, if you do not use this to supplement the fighting troops and allow others to deceive you, and say that you have been deceived by others, what else can be said? As for opening a bank in the name of adjusting the financial situation in Rehe and sending Gao to manage it, the people's hard-earned donations were originally intended to comfort the volunteer army, but now they are used to open a bank, which is a great violation of the original intention of the donations. You also provided a large amount of funds to Tang Yulin. At that time, there was no war in Rehe, and Tang did not send a single soldier to aid the anti-Japanese resistance in the Northeast for more than a year. When the Japanese invaders invaded Rehe, he abandoned the entire province of Rehe in just a few days. To send a large amount of funds to Tang Yulin, who retreated without a fight, instead of aiding the Northeast Army, which was actually resisting the Japanese, is truly incomprehensible. Du's department received 40,000 yuan in consolation money from you, sir, before and after. The receipt stated 'Chairman Zhu's reward.' At that time, it was thought that it was your personal money, and the soldiers were praised for their kindness. However, after arriving in Shanghai, it was learned that it was donated by compatriots at home and abroad and entrusted to you, sir, for distribution. This is just a small part of it. The above items are either based on solid evidence or heard from others, and are not fabricated by Du. In recent years, there have been famines and wars, and you, sir, have been running around to provide relief. Your kindness and compassion have won the trust of the people. I admire you in private and am filled with admiration. How dare I tarnish your reputation with greedy and stingy actions? However, what people are privately discussing, Du will speak out plainly to resolve doubts and use it as a straightforward statement. Because of my deep love, I do not realize that my words are earnest. You, sir, are appealing in the mainland, while Du is fighting on the frontier, both serving the country, with no personal opinions in between. I am now replying to your previous telegram. Li Du bows with coldness."

Zhu Yuqiao's Reply Telegram 101

Mr. Zhu Qinglan received Li Du's cold telegram late the day before yesterday, and replied to Li via telegram yesterday, explaining the facts of each question raised by Li. The original telegram is as follows: "Mr. Li Zhichu, with respect, I received your fast telegram at 11:30 PM on the 16th of this month and read it in full. I appreciate your indication that there was indeed a conversation with the newspaper, but the statement that Qinglan used 500,000 yuan in donations to run a school was a mishearing by the reporter. Also, the statement that a receipt for 10,000 yuan was issued but only 6,000 yuan was received refers to those in Beijing, Tianjin, and Shanghai who borrowed the name solely for propaganda, not that Du's department received the funds in this way. It seems that the content of your conversation published in the Jingbao on the 8th is completely untrue. It can be seen that hearsay is not to be easily believed. Your telegram said, 'Because of my deep love, my words are earnest,' which I greatly appreciate. I only regret that you, sir, have had repeated talks in Shanghai, but have never inquired about this, so that Qinglan could tell you the facts. Now that you have gone to Lushan, you are expressing your opinions through newspapers and telegrams, resulting in repeated errors or incomplete statements, which I deeply regret. Now, I will reply to each section raised in your telegram separately: (1) Your telegram said, '500,000 yuan in donations were used to open a bank in Rehe.' After investigation, this section is not true at all and is completely a misunderstanding. The reason for the misunderstanding is probably because the exchange rates in Rehe were stagnant last winter, and the original paper money of the Xingye Bank fluctuated constantly, causing financial chaos. The cash aid received by the volunteer armies on the Rehe border was difficult to exchange and use. If this problem was not resolved, there could be internal unrest in Rehe at any time without the enemy attacking. Qinglan once asked Minister Song and the central government, as well as the China and Jiaotong Banks, to set up branches in Rehe to provide relief. After consultation, it was decided to have the Fuli Bank go to add branches and fulfill the obligation of exchange and turnover. The establishment of this bank was long before ten years ago and had nothing to do with Qinglan. The establishment of branches by this bank has nothing to do with the donations. There are facts to investigate. (2) Your telegram said, 'The central government allocated 400,000 yuan to aid the anti-Japanese armies in the Northeast, and you, sir, sent a batch to Tang Yulin to manufacture 40,000 sets of leather military uniforms and transport them to Rehe.' After investigation, this section is even more untrue. Qinglan has never sent any funds to Tang to manufacture leather military uniforms. All funds from the central government to aid the anti-Japanese armies in the Northeast have accounts and records to check. I do not know what the above statement is based on. (3) Your telegram said, 'Guns and cannons worth more than 800,000 yuan were purchased and stored in Beiping.' After investigation, this section is even more shocking to hear. 800,000 yuan is a huge amount. To use it to purchase a large number of guns and cannons, how could any private individual be able to handle its transportation and storage? Where did this statement come from? Please clearly indicate where it is stored in Beiping. (4) Your telegram said, 'It was discovered in Tianjin that people from the office of you sir were privately selling ammunition, and many were arrested and are still in custody.' After investigation, this section is almost incredibly ridiculous. Since they have been arrested and are still in custody, please provide the names of those arrested, where they are being held, and whether they are from Qinglan's office. (5) Your telegram said, 'Yang Binlou and Gao Bosheng went to the Northeast on your orders to contact various military units.' After investigation, this section does not match the facts. Yang Binlou returned to the Northeast last year on his own initiative to work in Shanghai and requested assistance. He was not sent by Qinglan. Therefore, Qinglan telegraphed back to you, sir, saying that he knew of such a person, but he was not Qinglan's representative. Otherwise, when he left, a certificate letter would have been issued. As for Gao Bosheng, I have never known him. (6) Your telegram said, 'Since the incident, many people in Beijing, Tianjin, and Shanghai have been borrowing the name of anti-Japanese resistance to engage in propaganda work and have received more consolation money, while those who actually resist the Japanese have not benefited. I ask, who should be held responsible?' Who are those who are borrowing the name? Where did they get more consolation money? Who are those who are actually resisting the Japanese? What kind of benefits should they receive? Please point out the facts, and the responsibility will be clear. (7) Your telegram said, 'The Jilin army was hungry and cold and transferred battles, and the expected clothing expenses of 200,000 yuan could not be obtained in full, resulting in defeat.' After investigation, your representative, Mr. Wang Ziyao, requested 200,000 yuan for clothing expenses last autumn. At that time, in addition to requesting the government to provide assistance, I repeatedly appealed to the society and introduced your representative to contact various circles. As a result, only 20,000 yuan was raised in Shanghai and remitted. The fact that this was the process can be confirmed by letters and telegrams. Qinglan sincerely apologizes for not being able to provide widespread assistance to the anti-Japanese armies in the Northeast. But Qinglan has done his best, and what cannot be done is limited to Qinglan's ability. Those who are understanding should be able to understand this. (8) Your telegram said, 'The central government allocated ammunition to you, sir, but you did not replenish it. You also made a large number of military uniforms and purchased a large number of guns and cannons. This is why there are rumors that you, sir, were planning your own development.' After investigation, the central government has never had ammunition delivered to Qinglan to be designated for transfer to your department. Moreover, your department is far away in Sanxing, in an isolated area, making it impossible to transport. As for the military uniforms made by Qinglan, they were all worn by officers and soldiers of the Jilin, Heilongjiang, and returned to Rehe volunteer armies. Otherwise, they would not have been able to survive the cold winter and spring. The statement about purchasing a large number of guns and cannons has been answered in detail in the third section. Where did the statement about planning your own development come from? (9) Your telegram said, 'Your department received 40,000 yuan in consolation money from Qinglan before and after. The receipt stated "Chairman Zhu's reward".' After investigation, all the funds that Qinglan gave to your department were received by your representative Wang Ziyao (named Zhirong). The receipts are available and there has never been a so-called payment slip with the words 'Chairman Zhu's reward'. This can be thoroughly investigated. In short, you, sir, have just returned from overseas and may not be familiar with the past. You, sir, also know that donation income is collected sporadically, and no matter when, large amounts cannot be accumulated. How could there be a saying that there are more than 3 million yuan in savings in Shanghai? Moreover, there are many volunteer armies in various places, so how can the limited donations be able to provide universal and sufficient assistance? As the saying goes, 'A team of horses cannot catch the tongue.' It is hoped that you, sir, will investigate the facts in detail for anything heard. This is my sincere hope. Zhu Qinglan bows."

The Local Association Replies to the Investigation Committee 102

Has Never Managed the Income and Expenditure of National Salvation Donations

The Shanghai All Circles Investigation Committee for National Salvation Donations sent letters to various public organizations in Shanghai that handled national salvation donations, requesting them to submit all account books and receipts by the 23rd of this month for investigation. This has been reported in this newspaper. It is now known that the Shanghai Local Association has also received the above letter.
